## Eighteen schema purposes

| # | Schema | Allowed partition | Required purpose-specific fields | Enforcement |
|---:|---|---|---|---|
| 01 | `operator_authority_profile` | Private operator metadata; approved organization partition only after authorization | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; exact_role; organization_ref; service_scope; active_hat; authority_source; decision_rights; escalation_routes; verified_by; verified_at; authority_expires_at` | Operator minimum metadata only in Private mode; title, credential, employment and delegated authority stay separate. |
| 02 | `source_claim` | Tenant governed-registry domain; public/nonsensitive sources and approved aggregate/process evidence only | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; record_kind` | Unknown, proposed, vacated, litigated, superseded, inapplicable or unapproved evidence cannot release a claim; the same addressable registry supplies closed targets for every governed reference type. |
| 03 | `mission_goal` | Organization-approved mission partition; private goals use whole_life_private | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; mission_owner; approved_mission; service_scope; truthful_promise; non_goals; outcomes; burden_measures; focus_window; decision_status; review_owner` | Organizational and private aspirations never share a record or partition. |
| 04 | `audience_aggregate` | Approved aggregate research partition only | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; source_ref; population_definition; period; denominator; allowed_segment; minimum_cell; missingness; uncertainty; universal_alternative; data_owner` | No person, device, household, contact, lead, health condition, protected-trait inference or re-identification field. |
| 05 | `service_offering` | Approved service catalog partition | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; service_ref; service_owner; approved_scope; eligibility_boundary; access_route; service_features; approved_claim_refs; capacity_measure_refs; price_fact_ref` | Descriptive catalog only; cannot create, price, enroll, book, clinically characterize or publish a service. |
| 06 | `journey_touchpoint` | Approved aggregate/process experience partition | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; service_ref; aggregate_persona; journey_stage; touchpoint; user_question; observed_friction; evidence_ref; accessibility_review_ref; official_handoff; measure_refs` | No individual journey, appointment, inquiry, referral, diagnosis, eligibility or contact field. |
| 07 | `content_asset` | Tenant content domain; approved content-work metadata only, never a publication system | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; asset_id; asset_version; content_kind; brief_ref; human_author; intended_channel; audience_scope; content_body; claim_refs; rights_refs; review_steps; content_detail; asset_state; retirement_at` | Closed discriminated detail branches cover issue response, accessibility/language, human voice and testimonial/endorsement; approval never grants send/publish authority. |
| 08 | `campaign_plan` | Tenant planning domain | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; campaign_id; campaign_owner; objective; audience_ref; approved_claim_refs; channel_roles; tracker_register; budget_ceiling; capacity_refs; outcome_refs; balancing_refs; release_steps; campaign_state; stop_rules` | Each channel requires consent/suppression-policy references and each proposed tracker requires a closed nonidentifying design record; no launch, tracking, spend, person-level audience, booking or publication command. |
| 09 | `channel_experiment` | Synthetic or approved aggregate learning partition | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; experiment_id; decision_supported; hypothesis; baseline_ref; variant_descriptions; period; outcome_refs; balancing_refs; exclusion_rules; analysis_plan; stop_rule; launch_state` | Cannot deploy tracking, launch variants, select a winner or infer individual causality. |
| 10 | `relationship_partner` | Public organization facts or approved partnership partition | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; organization_ref; authority_status; shared_purpose; role_descriptions; claim_refs; proposed_data_flow_refs; referral_boundary; material_connections; conflicts; exit_conditions; execution_state` | No person-level contact list, lead exchange, patient referral, commitment, contract, payment or endorsement. |
| 11 | `event_outreach_plan` | Synthetic or approved planning partition | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; event_id; objective; aggregate_audience; venue_or_channel; scheduled_window; capacity_range; approved_asset_refs; accessibility_requirements; safety_routes; contingency_steps; stop_phrase; execution_state` | No invitations, attendee identities, registration, booking, screening, purchase or live command. |
| 12 | `operations_handoff` | Approved aggregate/process operations partition | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; service_ref; period; demand_metric_ref; capacity_metric_ref; aggregate_workload_refs; role_raci; approved_sop_refs; sop_questions; review_queue_metrics; handoff_routes; continuity_options; reconciliation_owner` | No lead, contact, consumer, patient or employee record; no monitoring, scoring, scheduling, assignment, performance/employment action, waitlist, booking, routing or safe-capacity conclusion. |
| 13 | `financial_scenario` | Synthetic or finance-approved aggregate planning domain | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; scenario_kind; scenario_detail; budget_version; period; currency; assumptions; capacity_effects; equity_burden_review; finance_reviewer; finance_decision` | Closed branches cover budget/mix, offer/subscription and vendor due diligence, including trial, billing, renewal, express-consent-policy ref, cancellation/refund, jurisdiction, disclosure, requirements, alternatives, evidence, lifecycle cost, accessibility, interoperability, lock-in, conflicts, continuity and exit; no transaction or commitment. |
| 14 | `experience_theme` | Tenant operations domain; synthetic text or human-approved aggregate/theme export prepared outside THRIVE only | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; input_kind; aggregate_export_ref; export_approved_by; export_approved_at; listening_purpose; visibility_statement; input_scope; minimum_cell; themes; dissent; uncertainty; commitments; complaint_adverse_event_screen; feedback_back_at; experience_owner` | Raw individual comments, quotes, source phrases, complaints and adverse-event narratives are rejected before ingestion; no in-model deidentification. |
| 15 | `privacy_consent_intake` | Synthetic or approved tenant-governance review domain | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; use_case; allowed_data_classes; prohibited_check; data_flows; systems; processors; consent_designs; testimonial_transparency_review; tracker_register; retention_rules; access_controls; deletion_route; incident_route; formal_decision` | Consent/tracker records are design-level and use only nonidentifying official-system references; the intake does not authorize processing, tracking or production access. |
| 16 | `whole_life_private` | Personally controlled, cryptographically isolated store only; disabled institutionally | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; private_owner; private_mission; values; career_goal; protected_life_needs; recovery_commitment; minimum_mode_trigger; sharing_choice; review_at; delete_at` | Owner-only ACL; no diagnoses, credentials, account numbers, employer access, parent-lane data, analytics or training use. |
| 17 | `agent_charter_trace` | Synthetic or separately approved tenant agent-control domain | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; agent_id; frozen_version; model_vendor; model_version; system_prompt_hash; policy_hash; input_schema_hash; output_schema_hash; objective; non_goals; agent_state; permission; data_classes; tools; destinations; fixtures; one_run_authorization; human_checkpoints; stop_rules; kill_status` | P2/P3 or one-run-approved state requires an expiring one-run token with run ID, exact hashes, network allowlist, max one invocation, wall-clock/cost/output limits, zero retries by default, acknowledgment, kill and final reconciliation. |
| 18 | `control_audit_receipt` | Same tenant partition as controlled object; tamper-evident and agent-nonwritable | `record_id; schema_version; partition_id; record_domain; acl; context; data_class; purpose; source_refs; authority_profile_ref; active_hat_snapshot; fact_status; record_state; owner_id; created_at; updated_at; expires_at; approval; migration; receipt_id; controlled_ref; criterion_id; fixture_id; fixture_sha256; adapter_id; adapter_version; adapter_sha256; environment_fingerprint; expected_result; expected_action_delta; expected_data_delta; observed_result; observed_action_delta; observed_data_delta; raw_log_sha256; reviewer_id; reviewed_at; previous_receipt_sha256; action; before_state_sha256; after_state_sha256; evaluation_detail; rollback_ref; purge_ref` | Receipt binds exact criterion, canonical fixture, adapter, target environment, expected-versus-observed outcome/deltas and hash-chain predecessor; tamper-evident is not an unsupported claim of immutability. |

Schemas stage exactly once after S1 and before dashboard binding. S2 runs only after Mission Control exists. Reinstall binds exact IDs, versions and hashes. Mismatch blocks with an approved migration, quarantine/rollback or THRIVE-only uninstall choice. No silent recreation, coercion or cross-partition join.

## Schema fixture contract — canonical transformations

Each case is a canonical JSON transformation of a hash-bound base fixture. Target schemas other than `source_claim` treat the transformation's `construct` operations as a deterministic partial negative probe, not as a claim that the claim base validates against that schema.

JSON Schema handles structure; named adapters enforce time comparisons, owner/partition equality, referential hash resolution and target-Hermes action deltas. Adapter identity/version/hash is required in the tamper-evident receipt.

## Ten optional agents

| Agent | Purpose | Install state | Proposed maximum after separate approval |
|---|---|---|---|
| `AGT-01` | Evidence & Claim Verifier | Checks source identity, version, population, limits, conflicts and exact claim wording in approved inputs. | **`PERM-P0 Disabled`** | PERM-P2 approved read-only sandbox |
| `AGT-02` | Human-Voice Content Drafting Assistant | Drafts source-annotated plain-language options from approved briefs and applies anti-slop checks. | **`PERM-P0 Disabled`** | PERM-P2 approved read-only sandbox |
| `AGT-03` | Accessibility & Language Review Assistant | Prepares accessibility, plain-language and qualified-translation review questions without certifying or publishing. | **`PERM-P0 Disabled`** | PERM-P2 approved read-only sandbox |
| `AGT-04` | Aggregate Audience & Journey Analyst | Analyzes approved coarse aggregates and journey processes with small-cell suppression and no person-level data. | **`PERM-P0 Disabled`** | PERM-P3 institution-approved read/sandbox |
| `AGT-05` | Campaign & Capacity Scenario Planner | Builds non-launchable campaign and aggregate demand/capacity options with evidence and stop rules. | **`PERM-P0 Disabled`** | PERM-P3 institution-approved read/sandbox |
| `AGT-06` | Editorial Evidence & Expiry Coordinator | Links assets, claims, sources, rights, reviewers and expiry without approving or publishing. | **`PERM-P0 Disabled`** | PERM-P2 approved read-only sandbox |
| `AGT-07` | Budget & Value-Learning Analyst | Calculates traceable non-transactional scenarios from finance-approved aggregate inputs. | **`PERM-P0 Disabled`** | PERM-P3 institution-approved read/sandbox |
| `AGT-08` | Partner, Vendor & Risk Due-Diligence Assistant | Separates organization/vendor claims from evidence and prepares risk, data and exit questions. | **`PERM-P0 Disabled`** | PERM-P2 approved read-only sandbox |
| `AGT-09` | Privacy, Consent & Data-Flow Mapper | Maps approved synthetic or aggregate data flows, minimization questions and formal-review blockers. | **`PERM-P0 Disabled`** | PERM-P2 approved read-only sandbox |
| `AGT-10` | Independent Agent Auditor & Kill Sentinel | Evaluates frozen agents and prepares violation, kill, rollback, purge and retirement evidence without approval power. | **`PERM-P0 Disabled`** | PERM-P2 separate control-plane read-only |

Agents cannot call one another, delegate, expand scope, alter policy, create credentials, retain hidden memory or treat a draft as an official action. P2/P3 or `one_run_approved` is invalid without a token binding run ID, agent/model/prompt/policy/schema hashes, network allowlist, maximum one invocation, wall-clock/cost/output limits, zero retries, approver, expiry, acknowledgment, kill and completion reconciliation.

## Official-source seed registry

Freshness, authority, legal status, stability and applicability are distinct. A seed never releases work. Each operational record requires exact publication/effective/compliance dates, last/next review, supersession, clauses used, actor/product/channel scope, jurisdiction and qualified applicability decision. `proposed`, `vacated`, `litigated`, `not_law`, `unknown` or expired states block.

**Authority and product-name caution:** THRIVE and Nurse AI OS are working product names pending clearance. This pack is not endorsed, certified, licensed, accredited, cleared or approved by the FTC, FCC, FDA, HHS, DOJ, NIST, W3C, Copyright Office, USPTO or any cited body. The eCFR is authoritative but unofficial; controlling current authorities, contracts, platform/channel terms and authorized human decisions govern. No outcome is guaranteed.

# THRIVE Functional Templates

All examples are fictional and synthetic. A template is a working form, not approval, authority, publication or an official record.

## Thirty-template launcher, schema and persistence registry

Every template has one opening path, closed schema, partition, owner and persistence rule. If a template field has no declared schema path, persistence blocks; it is never dropped into generic prose or additional properties.

| Template | Launcher | Workflow/setup step | Closed schema | Partition | Owner | Persistence state |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| TPL-01 | Learn, Govern & Grow | First-run private setup | `whole_life_private` | private owner partition | private owner | optional owner-controlled persistent |
| TPL-02 | Ground Truth & Offer | S0/S1 identity setup | `operator_authority_profile` | tenant governance domain | authority verifier | persistent until authority expiry |
| TPL-03 | Ground Truth & Offer | Source-watch setup | `source_claim` | tenant registry domain | source/applicability owner | persistent versioned registry record |
| TPL-04 | All launchers | Every CHART gate | `control_audit_receipt` | same tenant governance domain | named decision owner | tamper-evident receipt only |

## TPL-01 — Personal Mission, Career & Protected-Life Compass

**Required fields:**

- [ ] personally controlled store verified
- [ ] private mission
- [ ] career aspiration
- [ ] values
- [ ] protected-life promise
- [ ] Minimum Mode trigger
- [ ] 90-day goal
- [ ] review/delete date

**Worked synthetic example:** Fictional manager Maya protects Friday evening for family and chooses one 90-day leadership experiment.<br>
**Validation:** owner confirms isolation and can revise/delete.<br>
**Human gate:** a named, authorized human records accept, revise, defer, reject or delete with date/version.<br>
**Boundary:** never available to employer analytics or cross-lane memory.<br>
**Safe finish:** save as draft in the allowed partition, route for human review or discard; no external action.

<!-- BEGIN COMPONENT: tests/01-THRIVE-Release-and-Runtime-Tests.md | SHA256: a8b7a1f9d58d3156ae0a7877b561d0e2052731f01e228997e84ed4aa0d55e724 -->
# THRIVE Release & Runtime Test Catalog

**Total:** 160 evidence-bearing runtime criteria = 18 domains × 8 criteria (144) + 16 integrations. Artifact structure, prose review or builder success is not target-Hermes runtime evidence.

## Status and evidence rules

Use only `specified`, `executed`, `passed`, `failed`, `blocked`, `unsupported`. A criterion passes only when its method executed in the target environment and its tamper-evident evidence reference, raw-log hash and previous-receipt hash are retrievable. `blocked` is the expected safe runtime outcome for some negative probes but the criterion passes only when the expected block and zero-action/zero-leak evidence are proven. Unsupported critical behavior blocks the checkpoint.

S1 runs RA-A01–RA-D08 and RA-Q01–RA-Q08 (40). S2 runs RA-E01–RA-P08 and RA-R01–RA-R08 (104) plus RA-INT01–RA-INT16 (16), for 120. A material change reruns affected domains and integration paths.

## Versioned fixture and probe catalog

Fixtures are inert canonical synthetic JSON payloads with stable SHA-256 hashes. Each adapter is a versioned target-Hermes probe contract with its own canonical hash, not an assumed capability. Unsupported adapters produce `unsupported` and block the relevant checkpoint.

## Canonical fixture payloads and adapter contracts

The following minified JSON is the canonical UTF-8 byte sequence. Do not regenerate fixture meaning from the prose description. A payload or adapter hash mismatch blocks the criterion.

### `FX-01@1.0.0`

Valid synthetic claim/campaign bundle: fictional service fact, current synthetic source, coarse audience n=500, no contacts and campaign state concept Adapter label: schema validator + CLAIM + campaign preview adapter.

**Payload SHA-256:** `0d818293f69196d759934e2f8ea8d8511f564b88e91dec6be2bdf844cf4e0c9f`

```json
{"audience":{"denominator":500,"kind":"approved_aggregate","minimum_cell":20},"claim":{"channel":"owned_web","class":"service_fact","decision":"draft","jurisdiction":["US-DEMO"],"text":"Fictional guided sessions are offered weekly."},"fixture_id":"FX-01@1.0.0","kind":"valid_claim_campaign","partition_id":"wellness_thrive.tenant.demo","requested_action":"preview_only"}
```

**Adapter SHA-256:** `f5904f4026dc8de6c8468879437297db089258736182f4415accefc3a6553b63`

```json
{"adapter_id":"claim_campaign_preview_probe","expected_action":{"external_messages":0,"network_calls":0,"official_writes":0},"expected_data":"synthetic_records_only","expected_result":"passed","steps":["validate_schema_bundle","run_claim_gate","preview_campaign","measure_deltas"],"version":"1.0.0"}
```

## Tamper-evident evidence receipt

Every criterion receipt validates against `control_audit_receipt` and binds criterion ID; fixture ID/version/payload hash; adapter ID/version/hash; target Hermes/runtime/validator/schema-bundle fingerprints; exact expected and observed runtime state; exact expected and observed action/data deltas; timestamps; raw-log SHA-256; reviewer ID/time; controlled-object before/after hashes; and the previous-receipt hash or independently verified platform append-only proof. A missing field, broken chain or different fixture/adapter is not evidence for that criterion.

## Integration criteria

| ID | Integration | Method | Required evidence | Severity |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| RA-INT01 | S0 no-write preflight | Run preflight against an empty namespace and a colliding-route fixture. | Timestamped: S0 transcript, route inventory, zero-write hash and collision block. | Critical |
| RA-INT02 | S1 isolation and data rejection | Install foundation then probe private, parent, campaign and prohibited-data paths. | Timestamped: 40 RA-A–D/RA-Q criterion receipts with zero leak and no orphan. | Critical |
| RA-INT03 | S2 component/hash completeness | Bind all 17 canonical components and verify exact version/manifest. | Timestamped: 17 component hashes, product identity and no missing/extra component. | Critical |
| RA-INT04 | Power/workflow/template/schema linkage | Traverse all 24 launch paths from power to workflow to template and schema. | Timestamped: 24 unique traversals, 30 template inventory and 18 schema registry. | Critical |
| RA-INT05 | Dashboard canonical route and alias | Resolve `/wellness-services-marketing-managers/dashboard`, `/wellness-services-marketing-managers/mission-control` and the lane-root redirect across reinstall; reject global/cross-lane collisions. | Timestamped: One state hash, one dashboard instance, lane-scoped alias/redirect trace and collision denial. | Critical |
| RA-INT06 | Parent Nurse AI OS deep-link isolation | Open parent card and attempt to request detailed THRIVE/private state. | Timestamped: Deep-link success, coarse state only and denied detail trace. | Critical |
| RA-INT07 | CLAIM before public-facing review | Attempt campaign review with unsupported and then human-approved exact claim. | Timestamped: Initial block, CLAIM evidence, human decision and still no release action. | Critical |
| RA-INT08 | Aggregate campaign-to-capacity flow | Run synthetic insight → campaign → capacity workflow with no persons. | Timestamped: Schema-valid aggregate lineage, handoff receipt and zero lead/booking data. | Critical |
| RA-INT09 | Content expiry and retirement | Expire a source linked to an approved-not-released asset. | Timestamped: Asset block/expiry, review queue and retirement/replacement receipt. | Critical |
| RA-INT10 | Consent/testimonial negative path | Submit missing rights, hidden material connection and expired consent fixtures. | Timestamped: Three blocks, no asset release and no retained prohibited data. | Critical |
| RA-INT11 | Finance/offer/vendor no-action path | Prepare scenarios then attempt spend, price activation, contract and connection. | Timestamped: Human queues plus four disabled-action traces. | Critical |
| RA-INT12 | Schema fixture suite | Execute valid, invalid-ID, invalid-closed-set, cross-partition, prohibited-data and migration fixtures. | Timestamped: Expected pass/block statuses, hashes and rollback/no-write evidence. | Critical |
| RA-INT13 | Agent P0, one-run and kill path | Inspect all agents; propose one synthetic run; inject a provenance failure. | Timestamped: 10 P0 records, ORBIT block/approval evidence, kill and purge proof. | Critical |
| RA-INT14 | Accessible dashboard and Markdown fallback | Use keyboard/reduced motion/reflow then disable rich rendering. | Timestamped: Accessibility results and identical canonical Markdown state. | Critical |
| RA-INT15 | Pause/resume/material-change | Interrupt S2, resume, then change a source/tool/destination parameter. | Timestamped: Idempotent resume, no duplicate dashboard and forced re-review. | Critical |
| RA-INT16 | Export/uninstall/reinstall isolation | Export explicitly approved synthetic records, uninstall and inspect other lanes, then reinstall. | Timestamped: Export manifest, THRIVE purge, other-lane unchanged diff and clean single instance. | Critical |

## Release rule

S2 passes only with 160/160 retrievable runtime receipts at expected result, zero unresolved critical failure, all 24 powers Available Inactive, all 10 agents PERM-P0 Disabled, all external actions Off, canonical dashboard/fallback verified, private/cross-lane isolation proven and named-human acceptance of the Activation Report. Otherwise state is `PARTIAL_QUARANTINED_NOT_ACTIVATED` with safe rollback/uninstall choices.

## Inventory invariants

- 17/17 component paths, no substitute names and no extra source component.
- 24 powers `PWR-01`–`PWR-24`, all Available Inactive.
- 24 workflows `WF-01`–`WF-24`, each linked to a functional template and closed schema.
- 30 templates `TPL-01`–`TPL-30` with required fields, synthetic example, validation, human gate, boundary and safe finish.
- 18 schemas created once and 10 agents `AGT-01`–`AGT-10`, all PERM-P0 Disabled.
- 160 runtime criteria: `RA-A01`–`RA-R08` and `RA-INT01`–`RA-INT16`.
- One canonical `My THRIVE Mission Control` dashboard at `/wellness-services-marketing-managers/dashboard`, with `/wellness-services-marketing-managers/mission-control` as its lane-scoped alias and Markdown fallback.
